   function ez_isclean( data ) {
    if (typeof data === 'undefined') { data = document.URL; }
    var re = /(([^&lt;&gt;()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^&lt;&gt;()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))(@|%2540|%40)((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))/;
    var isClean = !re.test(data);
    return isClean;
}

var ez_queue = new Array();
function sort_queue(a, b)
{
  if( a.priority &lt; b.priority ) return -1;
  else if( a.priority == b.priority ) return 0;
  else return 1;  
}
function execute_ez_queue()
{
  ez_queue.sort( sort_queue );

  for( var i in ez_queue )
  {
        if(typeof ez_queue[i].method != "undefined")
        {
            ez_queue[i].method.call( null );
        }
  }
}

var ez_ad_units = new Array();    
function ez_write_tag(d) {
    if(ez_isclean() &amp;&amp; d instanceof Array) {
        try {
            if(isAboveFold(d[1]))
            {
                var sname = d[1].replace(/-/g,"_");
                var slot_name = 'ezslot_'+eval('ezslotn_'+sname);
                var br1 = eval('ezslotb_'+sname);
                eval(slot_name).setTargeting("br1",br1);
            }
        }
        catch(err) {
        }
        ez_ad_units[ez_ad_units.length] = d;
        var ezcmd = "googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-"+d[1]+"-0');});";
        return ezcmd;
    }
    else {
        return "1+1";
    }
}
function isAboveFold(name) {
    var span = document.querySelector('span[id^="div-gpt-ad-'+name+'-"]');
    if (span !== null) {
        var adParent = span.parentNode;
        if (adParent !== null) {
            var adCoords = adParent.getBoundingClientRect();
            var winHeight = "innerHeight" in window ? window.innerHeight : document.documentElement.offsetHeight;
            var winWidth = "innerWidth" in window ? window.innerWidth : document.documentElement.offsetWidth;
            if (adCoords.bottom &lt;= winHeight &amp;&amp; adCoords.right &lt;= winWidth) {
                //adParent.style.border = "13px solid red";
                return true;
            }
        }
    }
    else {
        return false;
    }
    return false;
}
function in_array(needle, haystack) {
    var length = haystack.length;
    for(var i = 0; i &lt; length; i++) {
        if(haystack[i] == needle) return true;
    }
    return false;
}

        /* ---
         getComputedStyle() doesn't do what you think it does. To get styles dynamically added
         to elements by scripts, there is no unified cross-browser way to do it, so you have to 
         construct a string (like cssText in Chrome) and use that instead. FF/IE do not work
         --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- */
        function ezoGetCurrentStyles( element ) {
            if (typeof(__JASS) !== 'undefined' &amp;&amp; typeof(__JASS.isChrome) === 'function' &amp;&amp; __JASS.isChrome()) return window.getComputedStyle(element).cssText;
            var styles = window.getComputedStyle(element);
            var cssText = [];
            for (var prop in styles) {
                if (typeof(styles[prop]) === 'string' &amp;&amp; styles[prop] !== '') {
                    cssText[cssText.length] = (prop.replace(/[A-Z]/g, function(x) { return '-'+(x.toLowerCase())}))+': '+styles[prop];
                }
            }
            return cssText.join('; ')+';';
        }

        /* ---
         Moves every class from the body tag to the stylesheet_body element
         --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- */
        function ezoBodyEventListener() {

                });

                    $ezJQuery('#stylesheet_body').attr('class', newStyle);
                }
            }
            setTimeout(ezoBodyEventListener, ezoBELTime);
            ezoBELTime = ezoBELTime * 2;
        }

        var ezoBELTime = 10;
        var ezoOrigSBStyle = $ezJQuery('#stylesheet_body').attr('class');

function open_jquery_wrapper()
{

        old_jquery = jQuery;
        old_jquery_sign = $;
        $ = $ezJQuery;
        jQuery = $ezJQuery;
    }
}
function close_jquery_wrapper()
{
    if(typeof $ezJQuery != 'undefined')
    {
        $ = old_jquery_sign;
        jQuery = old_jquery;
    }
}

  <script language="javascript">
   (function ($) {
    var opt;
    $.fn.printThis = function (options) {
        opt = $.extend({}, $.fn.printThis.defaults, options);
        var $element = this instanceof $ ? this : $(this);

            var strFrameName = "printThis-" + (new Date()).getTime();

            if(window.location.hostname !== document.domain &amp;&amp; navigator.userAgent.match(/msie/i)){
                var iframeSrc = "javascript:document.write(\"&lt;he" + "ad&gt;&lt;scr" + "ipt&gt;document.domain='" + document.domain + "';&lt;/scr" + "ipt&gt;&lt;\/he" + "ad&gt;&lt;bo" + "dy&gt;&lt;\/bo" + "dy&gt;\")";
                var printI= document.createElement('iframe');
                printI.name = "printIframe";
                printI.id = strFrameName;
                printI.className = "MSIE";
                document.body.appendChild(printI);
                printI.src = iframeSrc;

            } else {
                 // other browsers inherit document.domain, and IE works if document.domain is not explicitly set
                var $frame = $("&lt;iframe id='" + strFrameName +"' name='printIframe' /&gt;");
                $frame.appendTo("body");
            }


            var $iframe = $("#" + strFrameName);

            // show frame if in debug mode
            if (!opt.debug) $iframe.css({
                position: "absolute",
                width: "0px",
                height: "0px",
                left: "-600px",
                top: "-600px"
            });


            var $result = null;
            var sep = (window.location.href.indexOf('?') &gt; -1) ? '&amp;' : '?';
            var scriptUrl = window.location.href + sep + "ez_orig=1";
            $.ajax({
               url: scriptUrl,
               type: 'get',
               dataType: 'html',
               async: false,
               success: function(data) {
                   $result = data;
               }
            });


        // $iframe.ready() and $iframe.load were inconsistent between browsers
        setTimeout ( function () {

            var $doc = $iframe.contents();

            //just get the ez_orig and pass it on
            //$doc.find("body").append($result);
            $iframe.get(0).contentWindow.document.open();
            $iframe.get(0).contentWindow.document.write($result);
            $iframe.get(0).contentWindow.document.close();

            var myInterval = setInterval(function () {

                if ($iframe.get(0).contentWindow.document.readyState == 'complete') {

                    clearInterval(myInterval);

                    if($iframe.hasClass("MSIE")){
                        // check if the iframe was created with the ugly hack
                        // and perform another ugly hack out of neccessity
                        window.frames["printIframe"].focus();
                        $doc.find("head").append("&lt;scr" + "ipt&gt; window.print(); &lt;/scr" + "ipt&gt;");
                    } else {
                        // proper method
                        $iframe.get(0).contentWindow.focus();
                        $iframe.get(0).contentWindow.print();
                    }

                    $element.trigger( "done");

                    //remove iframe after print
                    if (!opt.debug) {
                        setTimeout(function () {
                            $iframe.remove();
                        }, 1000);
                    }
                }

            }, opt.printDelay);

        }, 333 );

    };

    // defaults
    $.fn.printThis.defaults = {
        debug: false, // show the iframe for debugging
        importCSS: false, // import parent page css
        printContainer: false, // print outer container/$.selector
        loadCSS: "", // load an additional css file
        pageTitle: "", // add title to print page
        removeInline: false, // remove all inline styles
        printDelay: 500, // variable print delay S. Vance
        header: null // prefix to html
    };

    // $.selector container
    $.fn.outer = function () {
        return $($("&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;").html(this.clone())).html()
    }
})($ezJQuery);

{
    $ezJQuery('html').printThis();
};

    $ezJQuery.ajax({
        url: "/utilcave_com/bap.php?l="+lid+"&amp;p="+window.location.pathname+"&amp;d="+did,

            }
        },
        success: function(){

            $ezJQuery(el).closest('.ezoic-ad').parent().hide();
        }
    });
